msg:When we arrived there had just been an increase in covid cases in Beijing and as a result of this there was a demand from the province (Chongqing) for guests to have a PCR test done within the 48hours before checking in. We were unaware of this when we arrived. Fortunately I had been in communication with the concierge Jim regarding helping us organise a tour to Dazu, and as soon as Jim was made aware that we had arrived he came to the front desk. He arranged for our bags to be put away, and then took us down to the local clinic where he proceeded to arrange for us to have the test done. 
At a very crowded and busy test centre that was not easy to find, without Jim's help we would have struggled to find the clinic nevermind get the test done. Jim then also arranged that before we went upon our tour the next day that we would be able to go and collect our test results (which was just as well as entry to the dazu rock carvings was contingent upon having the test results). Jim was brilliant and went the extra mile to make sure we were taken care of from the moment we arrived to the moment that we left.

[Overall evaluation] The price/performance ratio is not high, but the location is irreplaceable. The decoration facilities are old, but the overall service level is in place. It is still a good choice to go during the off-peak season.

msg:Over the years, I have traveled all over the country and stayed in at least a hundred or so five-star hotels. This hotel should be ranked last in terms of cost-effectiveness among the hotels I have stayed in. 

The only reason I booked this hotel is that I have stayed in hotels of the same price or above in Jiefangbei, but not this one, just for the experience.
I didn't expect to be so disappointed.

Please believe my professionalism. This hotel is at most a little better than those express hotels, but the price is often four figures, so I say its cost-effectiveness is very low.
This hotel is very **, and it saves everything it can.
The lobby is very small, and there is not even a chandelier.
The decoration in the room seems very new, but there is almost no design, and it is all covered with uniform wallpaper. Strong express hotel style.
If you are used to staying in five-star hotels, you will feel that there is something missing here, which is actually the lack of decoration and design.
The room shown in the picture is very large, but in fact the room is very small. The size of this room is the size of the room in the express hotel.
If you look at the toiletries, toothpaste, etc., it is not much better than the express hotel.
The service staff missed such obvious garbage when cleaning. Please see the picture I uploaded.
You can never get through to the front desk by calling.

The only advantage is that it is very close to Jiefangbei, but it is not soundproof.
In such a busy city, the sound insulation of the glass is so poor.
At night, you can hear the sound from Jiefangbei and the sound of cars outside, even the sound of elevators in the corridor, and the sound of people talking.

It's very much like you have an old and small house and want to rent it out. You find someone to renovate it at the fastest speed and the lowest price, and then quickly make money.
It looks very new, but it's actually very bad. Such a hotel will show its true colors in 1-3 years at most.

If you are willing to stay in a fast hotel at the price of a five-star hotel, I admire your "magnificence".
If you are a normal person, I suggest you consider other hotels of the same price.
